      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Update conda and pip
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y
  WORKDIR /app
  # Copy environment files with CPU-only adjustments
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Create conda environment from environment_full.yaml (CPU-only, CUDA removed)
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Upgrade pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip==24.0
  # Install CPU-only PyTorch packages explicitly with pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir \
      torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  # Install pip requirements inside conda env (excluding CuPy and CUDA deps)
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  # Install viewer backend environment
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Install viewer backend pip requirements inside viewer conda env
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Copy entire repository content into /app
  COPY . /app
  # Ensure permissions
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  # Set PATH and environment for final shell
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  # Set entrypoint to bash shell in conda environment
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  # Install system dependencies with updated sources and required packages for VIPS
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Add backports repository for VIPS packages if necessary
  RUN echo "deb http://deb.debian.org/debian bullseye-backports main" > /etc/apt/sources.list.d/backports.list && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y -t bullseye-backports libvips-dev vips-tools && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (latest stable for x86_64 Linux)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Update conda and pip
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y
  WORKDIR /app
  # Copy environment files with CPU-only adjustments
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Create conda environment from environment_full.yaml (CPU-only, CUDA removed)
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Upgrade pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip==24.0
  # Install CPU-only PyTorch packages explicitly with pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir \
      torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  # Install pip requirements inside conda env (excluding CuPy and CUDA deps)
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  # Install viewer backend environment
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Install viewer backend pip requirements inside viewer conda env
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Copy entire repository content into /app
  COPY . /app
  # Ensure permissions
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  # Set PATH and environment for final shell
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  # Set entrypoint to bash shell in conda environment at /app
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  # Install system dependencies with updated sources and required packages for VIPS
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      vips-tools \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (latest stable for x86_64 Linux)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Update conda and pip
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y
  WORKDIR /app
  # Copy environment files with CPU-only adjustments
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Create conda environment from environment_full.yaml (CPU-only, CUDA removed)
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Upgrade pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip==24.0
  # Install CPU-only PyTorch packages explicitly with pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir \
      torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  # Install pip requirements inside conda env (excluding CuPy and CUDA deps)
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  # Install viewer backend environment
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Install viewer backend pip requirements inside viewer conda env
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Copy entire repository content into /app
  COPY . /app
  # Ensure permissions
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  # Set PATH and environment for final shell
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  # Set entrypoint to bash shell in conda environment at /app
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  # Install system dependencies with updated sources and required packages for VIPS
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Miniconda (latest stable for x86_64 Linux)
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  # Update conda and pip
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y
  WORKDIR /app
  # Copy environment files with CPU-only adjustments
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Create conda environment from environment_full.yaml (CPU-only, CUDA removed)
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Upgrade pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --upgrade pip==24.0
  # Install CPU-only PyTorch packages explicitly with pip inside conda env
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir \
      torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  # Install pip requirements inside conda env (excluding CuPy and CUDA deps)
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  # Install viewer backend environment
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  # Install viewer backend pip requirements inside viewer conda env
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  # Copy entire repository content into /app
  COPY . /app
  # Ensure permissions
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  # Set PATH and environment for final shell
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  # Set entrypoint to bash shell in conda environment at /app
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  RUN conda init bash
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  # Remove conda init bash, not needed in Dockerfile
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  # Separate conda update and pip install steps to isolate issues and pin conda version
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda install -n base -c defaults pip=24.0 -y && \
      conda clean -afy
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  WORKDIR /app
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -afy
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment_verbose.yaml environment_verbose.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  WORKDIR /app
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh

      conda env create -f environment_full.yaml
  RUN conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]

  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda install -n base conda=latest -c defaults -y
  RUN conda env create -f environment_full.yaml -v
  RUN conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml -v && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment_full.yaml environment_full.yaml
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda config --remove channels nvidia || true && \
      conda config --remove channels rapidsai || true && \
      conda env create -f environment_full.yaml -v && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml -v && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]

      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh

  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml -v && \
      conda clean -afy

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM python:3.10-slim-bullseye
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
      LANG=C.UTF-8 \
      LC_ALL=C.UTF-8 \
      PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH \
      CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      wget \
      bzip2 \
      ca-certificates \
      build-essential \
      git \
      curl \
      libglib2.0-0 \
      libsm6 \
      libxext6 \
      libxrender-dev \
      gdal-bin \
      libgdal-dev \
      openslide-tools \
      libvips-dev \
      python3-dev \
      python3-pip \
      python3-setuptools \
      python3-wheel \
      vim \
      less \
      zip \
      unzip \
      pkg-config \
      libffi-dev \
      libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH
  SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
  WORKDIR /app
  COPY environment.yaml environment.yaml
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml
  COPY requirements.txt requirements.txt
  COPY viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  RUN conda update -n base -c defaults conda -y && \
      conda config --set channel_priority strict && \
      conda config --add channels defaults && \
      conda config --add channels conda-forge && \
      conda config --add channels bioconda && \
      conda info && \
      conda config --show && \
      conda env create -f environment.yaml -v && \
      conda clean -afy
  SHELL ["conda", "run", "-n", "cellvit_env", "/bin/bash", "-c"]
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir torch==2.2.2+cpu torchvision==0.17.2+cpu torchaudio==2.2.2+cpu -f https://download.pytorch.org/whl/torch_stable.html
  RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt
  RUN conda env create -f viewer/SlideProvider/environment.yml -v && \
      conda clean -afy
  RUN conda run -n fastapi_patho pip install --no-cache-dir -r viewer/SlideProvider/requirements.txt
  COPY . /app
  RUN chmod -R a+rX /app
  ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DEFAULT_ENV=cellvit_env
  ENV CONDA_PREFIX=$CONDA_DIR/envs/cellvit_env
  WORKDIR /
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
  CMD ["-l"]
